# ui/pages/reports.py

import os
import datetime
import streamlit as st
from typing import List, Tuple, Type

# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# 1. 核心依赖
# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
from config import Config
from ui.utils import task_monitor  # 引入我们之前做好的双流监控器

# 引入报表文件管理器 (负责清理和打包)
from core.services.report_manager import ReportFileManager

# 引入所有业务分析服务 (逻辑核心，严格保持不变)
from core.services.sales_analyzer import SalesQtyAnalyzer
from core.services.profit_sku import SkuProfitAnalyzer
from core.services.profit_listing import ListingProfitAnalyzer
from core.services.profit_combo import ComboProfitAnalyzer
from core.services.crm import CustomerAnalyzer
from core.services.logistics import ShippingAnalyzer
from core.services.prediction import PredictionService
from core.services.ordering import OrderingService
from core.services.inventory_snapshot import InventorySnapshot


class ReportPage:
    """
    [UI层] 商业智能分析报告页面 (BI Reports) - Enterprise V2.0

    职责:
    1. 参数配置: 允许用户调整耗损率 (Loss Rates) 和 供应链参数 (Supply Chain)。
    2. 任务编排: 按顺序调用各个 Analyzer 服务。
    3. 进度反馈: 使用 task_monitor 实时展示后端日志和进度。
    4. 结果交付: 提供 ZIP 打包下载。
    """

    def __init__(self):
        self.report_manager = ReportFileManager()

        # 定义分析任务清单 (顺序执行)
        # 格式: (任务名称, 服务类)
        self.TASK_REGISTRY = [
            ("📦 SKU 销量统计 (Sales Analysis)", SalesQtyAnalyzer),
            ("💰 SKU 利润与诊断 (SKU Profit)", SkuProfitAnalyzer),
            ("🔗 Listing 表现分析 (Listing Profit)", ListingProfitAnalyzer),
            ("🎁 Combo 策略分析 (Combo Profit)", ComboProfitAnalyzer),
            ("👥 客户画像与风险 (CRM Analysis)", CustomerAnalyzer),
            ("🚚 物流效益诊断 (Logistics)", ShippingAnalyzer),
            ("🤖 AI 销量预测 (AI Prediction)", PredictionService),
            ("🛒 智能补货计算 (Smart Ordering)", OrderingService),
            ("🏦 库存资产快照 (Asset Snapshot)", InventorySnapshot)
        ]

    def _render_config_panel(self) -> dict:
        """
        [UI组件] 渲染参数配置面板
        """
        st.markdown("#### ⚙️ 业务参数配置 (Business Parameters)")
        st.caption("提示: 调整以下参数将直接影响 **净利润** 和 **建议补货量** 的计算结果。")

        with st.expander("展开详细参数设置", expanded=True):
            col_loss, col_supply = st.columns([1.2, 1])

            # 1. 耗损率配置 (Loss Rates)
            with col_loss:
                st.markdown("**📉 耗损率标准 (Loss Rates)**")
                # 读取 Config 当前值作为默认值
                lr_case = st.slider("投诉 (Case) 耗损率", 0.0, 1.0, Config.LOSS_RATES.get('CASE', 0.6), 0.01,
                                    format="%.2f")
                lr_req = st.slider("申请 (Request) 耗损率", 0.0, 1.0, Config.LOSS_RATES.get('REQUEST', 0.5), 0.01,
                                   format="%.2f")
                lr_ret = st.slider("退货 (Return) 耗损率", 0.0, 1.0, Config.LOSS_RATES.get('RETURN', 0.3), 0.01,
                                   format="%.2f")
                lr_disp = st.slider("争议 (Dispute) 耗损率", 0.0, 1.0, Config.LOSS_RATES.get('DISPUTE', 1.0), 0.01,
                                    format="%.2f")

            # 2. 供应链参数 (Supply Chain)
            with col_supply:
                st.markdown("**📦 供应链参数**")
                lead_time = st.number_input(
                    "订货提前期 (Lead Month)",
                    min_value=0.0,
                    value=float(Config.LEAD_MONTH),
                    step=0.1, format="%.1f",
                    help="从下单到入库预计需要的月数"
                )
                safety_month = st.number_input(
                    "最低安全库存 (Safety Month)",
                    min_value=0.0,
                    value=float(Config.MIN_SAFETY_MONTH),
                    step=0.1, format="%.1f",
                    help="为了防止断货保留的缓冲月数"
                )

        return {
            "loss_rates": {
                "CASE": lr_case, "REQUEST": lr_req, "RETURN": lr_ret, "DISPUTE": lr_disp
            },
            "lead_time": lead_time,
            "safety_month": safety_month
        }

    def _run_pipeline(self, start_date: datetime.date, end_date: datetime.date):
        """
        [核心逻辑] 执行全量分析流水线
        """
        # 构造文件名后缀 (e.g., 2025_10_01->2025_10_31)
        suffix = f"{start_date.strftime('%Y_%m_%d')}->{end_date.strftime('%Y_%m_%d')}"
        total_steps = len(self.TASK_REGISTRY)

        # 1. 清理旧报表
        self.report_manager.clear_old_reports()

        # 2. 启动监控器 (Task Monitor)
        with task_monitor(f"🚀 全量分析引擎启动 ({start_date} 至 {end_date})") as monitor:

            for idx, (task_name, ServiceClass) in enumerate(self.TASK_REGISTRY):
                step_index = idx + 1
                progress_pct = idx / total_steps

                # 更新主进度条
                monitor.update_main_progress(progress_pct)
                monitor.log(f"\n>>> [Step {step_index}/{total_steps}] 正在执行: {task_name}...")

                try:
                    # 实例化并运行 Service
                    # 注意: 这里严格传递了日期和后缀，逻辑与 V1.4.1 保持一致
                    service_instance = ServiceClass(start_date, end_date, suffix)
                    service_instance.run()

                    monitor.log(f" {task_name} 执行成功。")

                except Exception as e:
                    monitor.log(f" {task_name} 发生严重错误: {str(e)}")
                    # 打印堆栈以便调试 (在 UI 日志框中显示)
                    import traceback
                    monitor.log(traceback.format_exc())
                    # 我们选择不中断整个流程，让其他报表继续生成

            # 完成
            monitor.update_main_progress(1.0)
            st.session_state.analysis_finished = True

    def _render_download_zone(self):
        """
        [UI组件] 渲染下载区域
        """
        st.divider()
        st.subheader("📥 报表下载中心 (Download Center)")

        files = self.report_manager.get_generated_files()
        if not files:
            st.warning("⚠️ 未找到生成的报表文件，请检查上方日志是否有报错。")
            return

        # 生成 ZIP
        try:
            zip_bytes = self.report_manager.create_zip_archive()
            timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M')
            zip_filename = f"Eaglestar_Reports_{timestamp}.zip"

            col_zip, col_files = st.columns([1, 2])

            # 左侧: 大按钮下载 ZIP
            with col_zip:
                st.markdown("##### 📦 一键打包")
                st.download_button(
                    label="📥 下载所有报表 (.zip)",
                    data=zip_bytes,
                    file_name=zip_filename,
                    mime="application/zip",
                    type="primary",
                    use_container_width=True
                )

            # 右侧: 单文件列表
            with col_files:
                st.markdown("##### 📄 单文件下载")
                with st.expander("点击查看文件列表", expanded=False):
                    for f in files:
                        file_path = self.report_manager.get_file_path(f)
                        with open(file_path, "rb") as fp:
                            st.download_button(
                                label=f"📄 {f}",
                                data=fp,
                                file_name=f,
                                mime="text/csv",
                                use_container_width=True
                            )
        except Exception as e:
            st.error(f"打包文件时出错: {e}")

    def render(self):
        """
        [页面入口]
        """
        st.title("📊 商业智能报表 (BI Reports)")
        st.caption(f"Enterprise Analytics Engine {Config.APP_VERSION}")

        # --- 区域 1: 时间选择 ---
        with st.container(border=True):
            st.markdown("#### 📅 分析周期选择")
            c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
            with c1:
                # 默认上个月
                today = datetime.date.today()
                first_day_curr = today.replace(day=1)
                last_day_prev = first_day_curr - datetime.timedelta(days=1)
                first_day_prev = last_day_prev.replace(day=1)

                d_start = st.date_input("开始日期 (Start Date)", first_day_prev)
            with c2:
                d_end = st.date_input("结束日期 (End Date)", last_day_prev)

        # --- 区域 2: 参数配置 ---
        with st.container(border=True):
            params = self._render_config_panel()

        # --- 区域 3: 启动按钮 ---
        st.markdown("---")

        # 校验日期
        if d_start > d_end:
            st.error("⚠️ 开始日期不能晚于结束日期！")
            btn_disabled = True
        else:
            btn_disabled = False

        if st.button("🚀 确认参数并启动分析", type="primary", disabled=btn_disabled, use_container_width=True):
            # [关键步骤] 更新 Config (内存级更新，确保本次运行生效)
            Config.update_params(
                lead_time=params["lead_time"],
                safety_month=params["safety_month"],
                loss_rates=params["loss_rates"]
            )
            st.toast(" 参数已更新，引擎启动中...")

            # 初始化状态
            st.session_state.analysis_finished = False

            # 执行分析
            self._run_pipeline(d_start, d_end)

        # --- 区域 4: 结果展示 ---
        if st.session_state.get("analysis_finished", False):
            st.balloons()
            st.success("🎉 所有分析任务执行完毕！")
            self._render_download_zone()


def render():
    ReportPage().render()

# ui/pages/db_data_change.py

import streamlit as st
import pandas as pd
import time
from config import Config
from core.services.data_manager import DataManager


def verify_operator_password(input_pwd):
    """
    [安全组件] 校验运维操作密码
    用于高危操作 (High-Risk Actions) 的二次确认
    """
    if not Config.DB_OPERATOR_PWD:
        st.error(" 系统未配置操作密码 (DB_OPERATOR_PWD)，请联系管理员。")
        return False
    return input_pwd == Config.DB_OPERATOR_PWD


def render():
    st.title("🛠️ 数据修改中心 (Data Modification)")
    st.caption("允许授权用户手动修正库存数据或维护 SKU 基础资料。")

    # 初始化 Service
    mgr = DataManager()

    tab_inv, tab_cogs = st.tabs(["📦 修改库存 (Inventory)", "📝 资料维护 (Master Data)"])

    # =========================================================================
    # TAB 1: 修改库存 (Inventory) - 分步向导模式
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_inv:
        # 初始化 Session State
        if 'inv_mod_step' not in st.session_state: st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 1
        if 'inv_mod_date' not in st.session_state: st.session_state.inv_mod_date = None
        if 'inv_mod_sku' not in st.session_state: st.session_state.inv_mod_sku = None

        # --- Step 1: 选择月份 ---
        if st.session_state.inv_mod_step == 1:
            st.info("Step 1/3: 请选择要修改的月份列")
            cols = mgr.get_inventory_columns()

            if not cols:
                st.error("⚠️ 数据库中没有有效的月份列，请先上传库存文件。")
            else:
                sel_date = st.selectbox("选择日期列:", cols)
                if st.button("下一步 ➡️", key="btn_step1"):
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_date = sel_date
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 2
                    st.rerun()

        # --- Step 2: 选择 SKU ---
        elif st.session_state.inv_mod_step == 2:
            st.success(f"当前选中月份: **{st.session_state.inv_mod_date}**")
            st.info("Step 2/3: 请选择要修改的 SKU")

            all_skus = mgr.get_all_skus()
            sel_sku = st.selectbox("选择 SKU (支持搜索):", all_skus)

            c_back, c_next = st.columns([1, 5])
            with c_back:
                if st.button("⬅️ 返回"):
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 1
                    st.rerun()
            with c_next:
                if st.button("下一步 ➡️", key="btn_step2"):
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_sku = sel_sku
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 3
                    st.rerun()

        # --- Step 3: 修改数值并提交 ---
        elif st.session_state.inv_mod_step == 3:
            d = st.session_state.inv_mod_date
            s = st.session_state.inv_mod_sku

            st.markdown(f"#### 🎯 修改目标: `{s}` @ `{d}`")

            # 获取当前值
            curr_val = mgr.get_inventory_value(d, s)

            with st.container(border=True):
                c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
                with c1:
                    st.metric("当前库存", curr_val)
                with c2:
                    new_q = st.number_input("新库存数量", min_value=0, value=curr_val, step=1)

                st.markdown("---")
                pwd = st.text_input("🔑 请输入操作密码以确认修改:", type="password", key="pwd_inv_mod")

                c_submit, c_cancel = st.columns([1, 1])
                with c_submit:
                    if st.button("💾 确认保存", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                        if verify_operator_password(pwd):
                            ok, msg = mgr.update_inventory_qty(d, s, int(new_q))
                            if ok:
                                st.success(msg)
                                time.sleep(1.5)
                                # 返回第一步
                                st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 1
                                st.rerun()
                            else:
                                st.error(msg)
                        else:
                            st.error(" 密码错误，禁止修改。")

                with c_cancel:
                    if st.button("取消", use_container_width=True):
                        st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 2
                        st.rerun()

    # =========================================================================
    # TAB 2: 资料维护 (COGS) - 批量编辑 & 新增
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_cogs:
        mode = st.radio("操作模式:", ["📝 批量编辑 (Batch Edit)", "➕ 新增 SKU (Add New)"], horizontal=True)
        st.divider()

        # 准备下拉选项
        opt_cats = [""] + mgr.get_distinct_values('Category')
        opt_subs = [""] + mgr.get_distinct_values('SubCategory')
        opt_types = [""] + mgr.get_distinct_values('Type')

        # --- Mode A: 批量编辑 ---
        if mode == "📝 批量编辑 (Batch Edit)":
            st.info("💡 说明: 可直接在下方表格中修改 Cost 或 Freight，系统会自动计算 Cog。SKU 列不可修改。")

            # 加载数据 (使用 Session 缓存以支持即时计算)
            if 'df_cogs_edit' not in st.session_state:
                st.session_state.df_cogs_edit = mgr.get_cogs_data()

            # 编辑器组件
            edited_df = st.data_editor(
                st.session_state.df_cogs_edit,
                key="cogs_editor",
                use_container_width=True,
                height=500,
                column_config={
                    "SKU": st.column_config.TextColumn("SKU", disabled=True),
                    "Cog": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Cog (Auto)", disabled=True, format="%.2f"),
                    "Cost": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Cost", min_value=0, format="%.2f", required=True),
                    "Freight": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Freight", min_value=0, format="%.2f", required=True),
                    "Category": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("Category", options=opt_cats),
                    "SubCategory": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("SubCategory", options=opt_subs),
                    "Type": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("Type", options=opt_types),
                },
                hide_index=True
            )

            # 前端即时计算 (Reactive)
            # 检测数据是否变化，如果 Cost/Freight 变了，立即重算 Cog 并刷新 UI
            recalc_cog = (pd.to_numeric(edited_df['Cost'], errors='coerce').fillna(0) +
                          pd.to_numeric(edited_df['Freight'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)).round(2)

            if not edited_df['Cog'].equals(recalc_cog):
                edited_df['Cog'] = recalc_cog
                st.session_state.df_cogs_edit = edited_df
                st.rerun()

            # 提交区
            st.markdown("#### 💾 提交更改")
            c_pwd, c_btn = st.columns([1, 1])
            with c_pwd:
                pwd_edit = st.text_input("操作密码", type="password", key="pwd_cogs_edit", placeholder="请输入操作密码")
            with c_btn:
                st.write("")  # Layout spacer
                st.write("")
                if st.button("同步到数据库", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    if verify_operator_password(pwd_edit):
                        with st.spinner("正在同步..."):
                            ok, msg = mgr.update_cogs_batch(edited_df)
                        if ok:
                            st.success(msg)
                            # 强制刷新缓存
                            st.session_state.df_cogs_edit = mgr.get_cogs_data()
                            time.sleep(1)
                            st.rerun()
                        else:
                            st.error(msg)
                    else:
                        st.error(" 密码错误")

        # --- Mode B: 新增 SKU ---
        else:
            st.markdown("#### 🆕 录入新产品")
            st.warning("⚠️ 注意: 新增 SKU 会自动同步到库存表，所有历史月份库存默认为 0。")

            with st.container(border=True):
                c1, c2, c3 = st.columns(3)
                with c1:
                    n_sku = st.text_input("SKU (必填, 唯一)", placeholder="例如: AA-1234").strip()
                with c2:
                    n_cat = st.selectbox("Category", opt_cats, key="new_cat")
                with c3:
                    n_sub = st.selectbox("SubCategory", opt_subs, key="new_sub")

                c4, c5, c6 = st.columns(3)
                with c4:
                    n_type = st.selectbox("Type", opt_types, key="new_type")
                with c5:
                    n_cost = st.number_input("Cost", min_value=0.0, step=0.01, format="%.2f")
                with c6:
                    n_frt = st.number_input("Freight", min_value=0.0, step=0.01, format="%.2f")

                # 预览 Cog
                st.info(f"💰 预计 Cog: **{(n_cost + n_frt):.2f}**")

                st.markdown("---")
                pwd_add = st.text_input("操作密码", type="password", key="pwd_sku_add")

                if st.button("🚀 确认添加 SKU", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    if not n_sku:
                        st.error("SKU 不能为空")
                    elif not verify_operator_password(pwd_add):
                        st.error(" 密码错误")
                    else:
                        data = {
                            "SKU": n_sku, "Category": n_cat, "SubCategory": n_sub,
                            "Type": n_type, "Cost": n_cost, "Freight": n_frt
                        }
                        with st.spinner("正在写入..."):
                            ok, msg = mgr.add_new_sku(data)

                        if ok:
                            st.success(msg)
                            # 清理编辑缓存，确保切换回去能看到新SKU
                            if 'df_cogs_edit' in st.session_state:
                                del st.session_state.df_cogs_edit
                            time.sleep(1.5)
                            st.rerun()
                        else:
                            st.error(msg)

# ui/pages/db_admin.py

import os
import re
import time
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Dict, Tuple

import streamlit as st

# 确保 Config 被正确导入
from config import Config
from core.services.database_service import DatabaseService
from ui.components.safety import confirm_dangerous_action


def parse_filename_to_display(filename: str) -> str:
    """
    [UI辅助] 解析备份文件名 -> 人类可读格式
    Input:  20251205_174730_init.sql
    Output: 🕒 2025-12-05 17:47:30 | 🏷️ init
    """
    # 去掉路径，只取文件名
    filename = os.path.basename(filename)

    # 去掉扩展名
    base = filename.rsplit(".", 1)[0]
    parts = base.split("_", 2)

    if len(parts) >= 2:
        date_str, time_str = parts[0], parts[1]
        tag = parts[2] if len(parts) > 2 else ""

        # 严格校验是否为数字，防止解析非标准文件报错
        if date_str.isdigit() and time_str.isdigit():
            try:
                dt = datetime.strptime(date_str + time_str, "%Y%m%d%H%M%S")
                time_label = dt.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

                if tag:
                    return f"🕒 {time_label} | 🏷️ {tag}"
                else:
                    return f"🕒 {time_label}"
            except:
                pass

    # 如果解析失败，为了安全，不显示原始文件名，显示"未知备份"
    return "❓ 未知格式备份 (Unknown Backup)"


def _build_backup_options(file_list: List[str]) -> Tuple[List[str], Dict[str, str]]:
    """
    构建下拉菜单选项
    Returns: (UI显示列表, 映射字典{显示名: 物理文件名})
    """
    options_map = {}
    for f in file_list:
        display_name = parse_filename_to_display(f)
        # 如果有重复的时间点（极少见），追加后缀防止字典Key冲突
        if display_name in options_map:
            display_name += " (Copy)"
        options_map[display_name] = f

    # 按标签排序 (时间倒序，最新的在前面)
    sorted_labels = sorted(options_map.keys(), reverse=True)
    return sorted_labels, options_map


def render():
    st.title("🗄️ 数据库运维中心 (DB Admin)")
    st.caption("提供数据库快照备份、灾难恢复及环境重置功能。")

    service = DatabaseService()

    tab_backup, tab_restore, tab_manage, tab_danger = st.tabs([
        "📤 创建备份 (Backup)",
        "📥 灾难恢复 (Restore)",
        "🗂️ 备份管理 (Manage)",
        "☢️ 危险区域 (Danger Zone)"
    ])

    # =========================================================================
    # Tab 1: 创建备份
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_backup:
        st.info("💡 说明：此操作将为当前数据库的所有表创建全量快照 (System Snapshot)。")

        with st.container(border=True):
            c1, c2 = st.columns([3, 1])
            with c1:
                tag = st.text_input("快照备注 (可选)", placeholder="例如: Version_1.5_Update")
            with c2:
                st.write("")
                st.write("")
                if st.button("📸 立即备份", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    with st.spinner("正在生成快照..."):
                        ok, msg = service.create_backup(tag)
                    if ok:
                        st.success(msg)  # msg 在 service 层已经脱敏，只报大小
                        time.sleep(1)
                        st.rerun()
                    else:
                        st.error(msg)

    # =========================================================================
    # Tab 2: 灾难恢复 (安全脱敏)
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_restore:
        st.warning("⚠️ **高危警告**：还原操作将 **完全覆盖** 当前数据库，且不可撤销！")

        files = service.list_backups()
        if not files:
            st.info("暂无可用还原点。")
        else:
            labels, map_files = _build_backup_options(files)

            selected_label = st.selectbox("请选择还原时间点:", labels)
            # 获取物理文件名用于后端操作，但在前端隐藏
            real_filename = map_files[selected_label]

            st.divider()

            # [Fix] 安全组件：描述中使用 selected_label (格式化时间)，而非 real_filename
            confirmed, note = confirm_dangerous_action(
                title="🔴 最终确认：执行数据库回滚",
                description=f"即将还原至时间点: **{selected_label}**。\n请确认当前没有其他用户正在操作。",
                confirm_phrase="RESTORE",
                require_current_password=True,
                require_operator_password=True,
                key_prefix="db_restore"
            )

            if confirmed:
                progress_bar = st.progress(0.0, text="准备开始还原...")

                def update_ui(p):
                    progress_bar.progress(max(0.0, min(p, 1.0)), text=f"还原进度: {int(p * 100)}%")

                # 传递真实文件名给后端
                ok, msg = service.restore_backup_with_progress(real_filename, update_ui)

                if ok:
                    st.balloons()
                    st.success(f" 数据库已成功回滚至: {selected_label}")
                else:
                    st.error(msg)

    # =========================================================================
    # Tab 3: 备份管理 (安全脱敏)
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_manage:
        files = service.list_backups()
        if not files:
            st.info("暂无历史备份。")
        else:
            st.markdown("#### 🗑️ 历史快照管理")

            # [Fix] 表格展示：列出解析后的时间点，隐藏物理文件名
            df_files = []
            for f in files:
                try:
                    f_path = Config.BACKUP_DIR / f
                    size_kb = os.path.getsize(f_path) / 1024
                    display_name = parse_filename_to_display(f)

                    df_files.append({
                        "备份时间点 / 备注": display_name,
                        "文件大小": f"{size_kb:.1f} KB"
                    })
                except:
                    pass

            st.dataframe(df_files, use_container_width=True)
            st.markdown("---")

            # 删除操作区
            labels, map_files = _build_backup_options(files)
            target_label = st.selectbox("选择要删除的备份:", labels, key="del_sel")
            target_file = map_files[target_label]

            # [Fix] 按钮文本只显示时间点
            if st.button(f"🗑️ 删除: {target_label}", type="secondary"):
                ok, msg = service.delete_backup(target_file)
                if ok:
                    st.toast(f"已删除备份点: {target_label}")
                    time.sleep(1)
                    st.rerun()
                else:
                    st.error(msg)

    # =========================================================================
    # Tab 4: 危险区域 (Reset)
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_danger:
        st.error("💀 **极度危险区**：以下操作具有破坏性，请谨慎执行。")

        with st.container(border=True):
            st.markdown("#### 🧹 一键清空测试数据 (Reset Environment)")
            st.markdown(
                """
                此操作将 **永久清空** 以下业务数据表，仅保留用户账号和 SKU 基础资料：
                - 交易流水 (Transaction)
                - 资金流水 (Order Earning)
                - 报表源数据 (Clean Log)
                - 库存数据 (Inventory)
                """
            )

            confirmed, note = confirm_dangerous_action(
                title="⚠️ 确认清空业务数据",
                description="此操作不可撤销！建议先在 [备份] 页面创建一个快照。",
                confirm_phrase="RESET",
                require_current_password=True,
                require_operator_password=True,
                key_prefix="db_reset"
            )

            if confirmed:
                with st.spinner("正在重置数据库环境..."):
                    ok, msg = service.reset_business_data()

                if ok:
                    st.success(msg)
                    st.balloons()
                else:
                    st.error(msg)

# ui/pages/audit_logs.py
"""
安全审计日志查看页面 (Audit Logs Center) - Enterprise V2.3

Fix Log:
- UI增强: 在审计列表中显式增加 "来源 IP (Source IP)" 列，实现完整的操作溯源。
"""

from pathlib import Path
from typing import List, Dict, Any
import pandas as pd
import streamlit as st

from config import Config
from core.logging_config import get_logger

logger = get_logger(__name__)


# ==============================================================================
# 权限校验
# ==============================================================================
def _ensure_admin():
    user = st.session_state.get("auth_user")
    if not user or not user.get("is_admin"):
        st.error(" 权限不足：仅管理员可查看审计日志。")
        st.stop()
    return user


# ==============================================================================
# 日志解析引擎
# ==============================================================================
def _parse_log_line(line: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    解析标准日志格式:
    YYYY-MM-DD ... | user=X | action=Y | ... | ip=Z | Message
    """
    line = line.strip()
    if not line: return {}

    # 格式参考 core/logging_config.py
    # 使用 " | " 分割，最后一部分是 message
    parts = line.split(" | ")

    if len(parts) < 4:
        return {"time": "-", "level": "-", "user": "-", "ip": "-", "action": "-", "message": line}

    try:
        ts = parts[0].strip()
        level = parts[1].strip()
        module = parts[2].strip()

        message = parts[-1]
        kv_parts = parts[3:-1]  # 中间部分是键值对

        meta = {}
        for item in kv_parts:
            if "=" in item:
                k, v = item.split("=", 1)
                meta[k.strip()] = v.strip()

        return {
            "time": ts,
            "level": level,
            "module": module,
            "user": meta.get("user", "-"),
            "ip": meta.get("ip", "-"),  # 提取 IP
            "action": meta.get("action", "-"),
            "table": meta.get("table", "-"),
            "message": message,
            "raw": line
        }
    except:
        return {"time": "-", "level": "-", "user": "-", "ip": "-", "message": line}


def _load_logs(log_file: str, max_lines: int = 1000) -> pd.DataFrame:
    path = Path(Config.LOG_DIR) / log_file
    if not path.exists():
        return pd.DataFrame()

    try:
        with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore") as f:
            lines = f.readlines()[-max_lines:]
        lines.reverse()
        parsed_data = [_parse_log_line(l) for l in lines]
        return pd.DataFrame(parsed_data)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"读取日志失败: {e}")
        return pd.DataFrame()


# ==============================================================================
# 页面渲染
# ==============================================================================
def render():
    _ensure_admin()
    st.title("📜 安全审计日志 (Audit Logs)")
    st.caption("追踪系统内的所有敏感操作与数据变更，包含操作人 IP 溯源。")

    # --- 过滤器 ---
    with st.container(border=True):
        c1, c2, c3 = st.columns([1, 1, 1])
        with c1:
            log_source = st.radio("日志来源:", ["📢 业务操作日志 (Business)", "🛡️ 数据库底层日志 (DB Kernel)"])
        with c2:
            show_read = st.checkbox("显示只读操作 (SELECT/READ)", value=False)
        with c3:
            limit = st.select_slider("加载行数:", options=[100, 500, 1000, 2000], value=500)

    # --- 加载 ---
    filename = "app.log" if "Business" in log_source else "db_audit.log"
    with st.spinner(f"正在加载 {filename} ..."):
        df = _load_logs(filename, limit)

    if df.empty:
        st.info("暂无日志记录。")
        return

    # --- 过滤 ---
    df = df[df["action"] != "-"]
    if not show_read:
        mask_read = df["action"].str.upper().str.contains("READ|SELECT", na=False)
        df = df[~mask_read]

    search_term = st.text_input("🔍 搜索 (支持 User / IP / Action / Content):", placeholder="例如: 192.168 或 UPDATE")
    if search_term:
        mask_search = df.apply(lambda x: x.astype(str).str.contains(search_term, case=False).any(), axis=1)
        df = df[mask_search]

    st.markdown(f"**共找到 {len(df)} 条记录**")

    # --- [Fix] 表格展示：加入 IP 列 ---
    if "Business" in log_source:
        cols = ["time", "user", "ip", "action", "message"]
    else:
        cols = ["time", "user", "ip", "action", "table", "message"]

    st.dataframe(
        df[cols],
        use_container_width=True,
        hide_index=True,
        column_config={
            "time": st.column_config.TextColumn("时间", width="medium"),
            "user": st.column_config.TextColumn("操作人", width="small"),
            "ip": st.column_config.TextColumn("来源 IP", width="medium"),  # 新增列
            "action": st.column_config.TextColumn("动作", width="small"),
            "table": st.column_config.TextColumn("表名", width="small"),
            "message": st.column_config.TextColumn("详细内容 (Details)", width="large"),
        }
    )

    with st.expander("查看原始数据 (CSV Export)"):
        st.code(df.to_csv(index=False), language="csv")
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/audit_logs.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/pages/etl_cleaning.py ====================
# ui/pages/etl_ingest.py -> ui/pages/etl_cleaning.py
# (文件名保持一致: ui/pages/etl_cleaning.py)

import streamlit as st
import pandas as pd
import time
from core.repository.db_client import DBClient
from core.services.correction_service import CorrectionService
from core.etl.parser import TransactionParser


class DataCleaningPage:
    """
    [UI层] 数据清洗向导 (Data Cleaning Wizard) V1.5

    升级特性:
    1. 交互优化: 智能修复与手动录入互斥显示。
    2. 按需输入: 仅在手动模式下显示有问题的字段输入框。
    3. 严格校验: 提交前对 SKU 有效性和数量格式进行双重验证。
    """

    def __init__(self):
        self.db = DBClient()
        self.corrector = CorrectionService()

    def _run_auto_parser(self):
        """运行解析器并展示自动修复结果"""
        with st.spinner("🔄 正在重新扫描与自动修复..."):
            parser = TransactionParser()
            report = parser.run()

        if report.get("status") == "success":
            logs = report.get("auto_fixed", [])
            pending = report.get("pending_count", 0)

            if logs:
                st.success(f" 自动修复了 {len(logs)} 个历史问题！")
                with st.expander("查看修复详情", expanded=False):
                    for log in logs:
                        st.markdown(f"- 订单 `{log['order']}`: {log['msg']}")
            else:
                st.info("无自动修复项。")

            return pending
        return 0

    def _get_next_issue(self):
        """获取第一条待处理的异常记录"""
        # P_Flag=99 表示校验未通过
        sql = "SELECT * FROM Data_Transaction WHERE P_Flag = 99 LIMIT 1"
        df = self.db.read_df(sql)
        if df.empty:
            return None
        return df.iloc[0]

    def _find_first_bad_sku(self, row) -> dict:
        """在行中定位第一个错误的字段"""
        for i in range(1, 11):
            sku_col = f'P_SKU{i}'
            qty_col = f'P_Quantity{i}'

            sku_val = str(row[sku_col]).strip().upper()
            qty_val = str(row[qty_col]).strip()

            # 跳过空数据
            if not sku_val or sku_val == 'NONE': continue

            # 检查 SKU 是否有效
            is_sku_valid = self.corrector.is_valid_sku(sku_val)

            # 检查 数量 是否有效 (整数且大于0)
            is_qty_valid = self._is_valid_quantity(qty_val)

            # 只要有一个无效，就返回该组索引
            if not is_sku_valid or not is_qty_valid:
                return {
                    "index": i,
                    "bad_sku": sku_val,
                    "bad_qty": qty_val,
                    "is_sku_error": not is_sku_valid,
                    "is_qty_error": not is_qty_valid
                }
        return None

    def _is_valid_quantity(self, val: str) -> bool:
        """[辅助] 验证数量是否合法"""
        try:
            # 允许浮点数转整 (如 1.0 -> 1)，但不允许 0 或 负数
            v = float(val)
            return v > 0 and v.is_integer()
        except:
            return False

    def _commit_fix(self, order_id, col_idx, custom_label, bad_sku, bad_qty, correct_sku, correct_qty):
        """提交修复"""
        # 1. 记录记忆 (学习)
        self.corrector.save_correction(
            custom_label=custom_label,
            bad_sku=bad_sku,
            bad_qty=bad_qty,
            correct_sku=correct_sku,
            correct_qty=correct_qty
        )

        # 2. 更新数据库
        sku_col = f"P_SKU{col_idx}"
        qty_col = f"P_Quantity{col_idx}"

        sql = f"""
            UPDATE Data_Transaction 
            SET `{sku_col}` = :new_sku, `{qty_col}` = :new_qty
            WHERE `Order number` = :oid
        """
        self.db.execute_stmt(sql, {
            "new_sku": correct_sku,
            "new_qty": correct_qty,
            "oid": order_id
        })

        st.toast(f" 已修正: {correct_sku} x {correct_qty}")
        time.sleep(0.5)
        st.rerun()

    def render(self):
        st.subheader("🛠️ 数据清洗向导 (Data Cleaning Wizard)")

        col1, col2 = st.columns([3, 1])
        with col1:
            st.info("️ 系统将引导您逐个修复异常数据。您的选择将被系统记忆，下次自动应用。")
        with col2:
            if st.button("🔄 重新扫描全库", use_container_width=True):
                pending = self._run_auto_parser()
                if pending == 0:
                    st.success("🎉 数据已全部清洗完毕！")
                    time.sleep(1)
                st.rerun()

        # 1. 获取异常数据
        row = self._get_next_issue()
        if row is None:
            st.balloons()
            st.success("🎉 所有异常数据处理完毕！您可以进行下一步分析了。")
            return

        error_info = self._find_first_bad_sku(row)

        # 自愈机制: 如果标记了错误但找不到错，重置标记
        if not error_info:
            self.db.execute_stmt(
                "UPDATE Data_Transaction SET P_Flag=5 WHERE `Order number`=:oid",
                {"oid": row['Order number']}
            )
            st.rerun()
            return

        # 2. 提取上下文信息
        bad_sku = error_info['bad_sku']
        bad_qty = error_info['bad_qty']
        is_sku_error = error_info['is_sku_error']
        is_qty_error = error_info['is_qty_error']

        order_id = row['Order number']
        label = row['Custom label']
        title = row['Item title']

        # 3. 渲染界面
        with st.container(border=True):
            # 顶部信息栏
            st.markdown(f"### 🚩 发现异常: `{bad_sku}` (Qty: {bad_qty})")

            c_info1, c_info2 = st.columns(2)
            with c_info1:
                st.caption("Custom Label (原始标签)")
                st.code(label, language="text")
            with c_info2:
                st.caption("Item Title (商品标题)")
                st.info(title)

            st.divider()

            # --- 核心交互区 ---
            st.markdown("#### 🔧 选择修复方式")

            # A. 准备选项
            # 获取 SKU 建议
            suggestions = self.corrector.get_fuzzy_suggestions(bad_sku)

            # 构造单选框选项列表
            # 选项格式: "SKU_NAME" (隐含 Qty 沿用或默认1)
            # 始终包含 "手动修复" 作为最后一项
            radio_options = [s for s in suggestions]
            manual_option_label = "✍️ 手动录入 (Manual Input)"
            radio_options.append(manual_option_label)

            # B. 渲染单选框
            selected_option = st.radio(
                "请选择正确的数据:",
                options=radio_options,
                index=0,  # 默认选中第一个智能推荐
                horizontal=False
            )

            st.markdown("---")

            # C. 动态输入区 (State Machine)
            final_sku = None
            final_qty = None
            can_submit = False

            # 分支 1: 用户选择了 "手动录入"
            if selected_option == manual_option_label:
                c_in1, c_in2 = st.columns(2)

                # 只有 SKU 错才显示 SKU 输入框，否则显示只读
                with c_in1:
                    if is_sku_error:
                        input_sku = st.text_input("正确 SKU", value="", placeholder="请输入 Data_COGS 中存在的 SKU")
                    else:
                        input_sku = st.text_input("SKU (无需修改)", value=bad_sku, disabled=True)

                # 只有 Qty 错才显示 Qty 输入框
                with c_in2:
                    if is_qty_error:
                        input_qty = st.text_input("正确数量", value="1")
                    else:
                        input_qty = st.text_input("数量 (无需修改)", value=bad_qty, disabled=True)

                # 收集输入值
                final_sku = input_sku.strip().upper()
                final_qty = input_qty.strip()
                can_submit = True  # 手动模式下，点击按钮时再做最终校验

            # 分支 2: 用户选择了 "智能推荐"
            else:
                # 智能推荐选中的是 SKU
                final_sku = selected_option
                # 数量处理: 如果原数量是错的(例如N/A)，智能模式默认给1；如果是对的，沿用
                if is_qty_error:
                    final_qty = "1"
                    st.caption(f"💡 原数量 `{bad_qty}` 无效，智能修复将默认设为 `1`。")
                else:
                    final_qty = bad_qty

                can_submit = True

            # D. 提交按钮与处理
            if can_submit:
                if st.button(" 确认并修复 (Confirm & Fix)", type="primary", use_container_width=True):

                    # 最终校验逻辑
                    errors = []

                    # 1. 校验 SKU
                    if not final_sku:
                        errors.append("SKU 不能为空")
                    elif not self.corrector.is_valid_sku(final_sku):
                        errors.append(f"SKU `{final_sku}` 无效 (未在 Data_COGS 中找到)")

                    # 2. 校验 Quantity
                    if not self._is_valid_quantity(final_qty):
                        errors.append(f"数量 `{final_qty}` 无效 (必须是大于0的整数)")

                    # 执行或报错
                    if errors:
                        for e in errors:
                            st.error(f" {e}")
                    else:
                        # 格式化整数
                        clean_qty = str(int(float(final_qty)))
                        self._commit_fix(
                            order_id, error_info['index'],
                            label, bad_sku, bad_qty,
                            final_sku, clean_qty
                        )


def render():
    DataCleaningPage().render()
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/etl_cleaning.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/pages/ai_gemini.py ====================
# ui/pages/ai_gemini.py

import os
import time
import streamlit as st
import google.generativeai as genai
import requests
import datetime
from config import Config
from core.context import get_current_user
from core.services.chat_service import ChatService


# [Fix] 移除 _get_websocket_headers，使用 st.context.headers

def get_client_ip() -> str:
    """获取客户端 IP (st.context.headers)"""
    try:
        headers = st.context.headers
        if headers:
            if "Cf-Connecting-Ip" in headers: return headers["Cf-Connecting-Ip"]
            if "X-Forwarded-For" in headers: return headers["X-Forwarded-For"].split(",")[0].strip()
        session_info = st.runtime.get_instance().get_client_session_info()
        if hasattr(session_info, 'ip'): return session_info.ip
    except:
        pass
    return "UNKNOWN"


@st.cache_data(ttl=600)
def get_environment_context(ip: str) -> str:
    """获取环境上下文 (缓存)"""
    context_str = f"用户 IP: {ip}\n"
    if ip in ["UNKNOWN", "127.0.0.1", "localhost"]:
        return context_str + "位置: 本地开发环境 (未知位置)"
    try:
        loc_res = requests.get(f"http://ip-api.com/json/{ip}", timeout=2).json()
        if loc_res.get("status") == "success":
            city = loc_res.get("city", "Unknown")
            timezone = loc_res.get("timezone", "UTC")
            context_str += f"用户位置: {city} (时区: {timezone})\n"

            # 获取天气
            lat, lon = loc_res["lat"], loc_res["lon"]
            w_url = f"https://api.open-meteo.com/v1/forecast?latitude={lat}&longitude={lon}&current_weather=true&timezone={timezone}"
            w_res = requests.get(w_url, timeout=2).json()
            if "current_weather" in w_res:
                curr = w_res["current_weather"]
                context_str += f"当前天气: 气温 {curr['temperature']}°C\n"

            # 获取时间
            try:
                import pytz
                local_tz = pytz.timezone(timezone)
                now = datetime.datetime.now(local_tz).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
                context_str += f"当地时间: {now}\n"
            except:
                pass
    except:
        pass
    return context_str


def render():
    # 1. 初始化服务
    user = get_current_user() or "anonymous"
    chat_service = ChatService(user)

    # 2. API Key 检查
    api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_API_KEY")
    if not api_key:
        st.error(" 未配置 GOOGLE_API_KEY。")
        return

    # 3. CSS 优化 (让左侧列表更好看)
    st.markdown("""
        <style>
        .chat-row {
            padding: 10px;
            border-radius: 5px;
            margin-bottom: 5px;
            background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.05);
            transition: background-color 0.3s;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        .chat-row:hover {
            background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1);
        }
        .chat-active {
            background-color: rgba(78, 201, 176, 0.2) !important;
            border-left: 3px solid #4EC9B0;
        }
        </style>
    """, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    # 4. 布局：左侧历史，右侧对话
    col_sidebar, col_chat = st.columns([1, 3.5])

    # ===========================
    # 左侧：会话列表
    # ===========================
    with col_sidebar:
        if st.button("➕ 新建对话", use_container_width=True, type="primary"):
            chat_service.create_session()
            st.rerun()

        st.markdown("---")
        st.caption("🕒 历史记录")

        # 获取所有会话
        sessions = chat_service.get_all_sessions()
        active_info = chat_service.get_active_session()
        active_id = active_info["id"]

        # 渲染列表 (使用 container 增加滚动条效果)
        with st.container(height=600, border=False):
            for s in sessions:
                sid = s["id"]
                title = s["title"]
                is_active = (sid == active_id)

                # 使用列布局实现：标题 + 删除按钮
                c_text, c_del = st.columns([4, 1])

                # 标题按钮 (切换会话)
                # 这里的 key 必须唯一
                btn_type = "secondary" if not is_active else "primary"
                if c_text.button(f"💬 {title}", key=f"sel_{sid}", help=s["updated_at"], use_container_width=True,
                                 type=btn_type):
                    chat_service.set_active_session(sid)
                    st.rerun()

                # 删除按钮
                if c_del.button("🗑️", key=f"del_{sid}", help="删除此会话"):
                    chat_service.delete_session(sid)
                    st.rerun()

    # ===========================
    # 右侧：聊天窗口
    # ===========================
    with col_chat:
        current_session = active_info["data"]

        # 标题栏
        st.markdown(f"### 🤖 {current_session.get('title', 'Google Gemini')}")
        st.caption("Powered by Gemini 2.0 Flash | 🔒 独立记忆空间")

        # 获取环境上下文 (懒加载)
        if "ai_context_str" not in st.session_state:
            ip = get_client_ip()
            st.session_state.ai_context_str = get_environment_context(ip)

        # 初始化模型
        try:
            genai.configure(api_key=api_key)
            system_instruction = f"""
            你是一个专业的企业 ERP 智能助手 (Eaglestar ERP Assistant)。
            【当前用户环境信息】
            {st.session_state.ai_context_str}
            【你的职责】
            1. 回答关于库存管理、供应链、数据分析的通用问题。
            2. 保持回答简洁、专业。
            """
            model = genai.GenerativeModel(model_name='gemini-2.0-flash', system_instruction=system_instruction)
        except Exception as e:
            st.error(f"模型连接失败: {e}")
            return

        # 渲染消息流
        messages = current_session.get("messages", [])
        for msg in messages:
            with st.chat_message(msg["role"]):
                st.markdown(msg["content"])

        # 处理输入
        if prompt := st.chat_input("请输入您的问题..."):
            # 1. 记录用户消息
            chat_service.add_message(active_id, "user", prompt)
            with st.chat_message("user"):
                st.markdown(prompt)

            # 2. 生成回复
            with st.chat_message("assistant"):
                message_placeholder = st.empty()
                full_response = ""
                try:
                    # 构造上下文 (Gemini 格式)
                    chat_history = []
                    # 排除最新的一条用户消息，防止重复(如果是剛append的)
                    # 这里直接用 historic messages 构造 context
                    for m in messages:  # 历史消息
                        role = "user" if m["role"] == "user" else "model"
                        chat_history.append({"role": role, "parts": [m["content"]]})

                    chat = model.start_chat(history=chat_history)
                    response = chat.send_message(prompt, stream=True)

                    for chunk in response:
                        if chunk.text:
                            full_response += chunk.text
                            message_placeholder.markdown(full_response + "▌")

                    message_placeholder.markdown(full_response)

                    # 3. 记录助手回复
                    chat_service.add_message(active_id, "assistant", full_response)

                    # 如果是第一轮对话，刷新页面以更新左侧标题
                    if len(messages) == 0:
                        st.rerun()

                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"AI 响应异常: {e}")
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/ai_gemini.py ====================


==================== START FILE: tools/check_models.py ====================
# tools/check_models.py
import os
import google.generativeai as genai
from dotenv import load_dotenv

# 加载 .env 环境变量
load_dotenv()

api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_API_KEY")

if not api_key:
    print(" 错误：未找到 GOOGLE_API_KEY，请检查 .env 文件")
else:
    genai.configure(api_key=api_key)
    print("🔍 正在查询可用模型列表...\n")

    try:
        count = 0
        for m in genai.list_models():
            if 'generateContent' in m.supported_generation_methods:
                print(f" 模型名称: {m.name}")
                print(f"   描述: {m.description}")
                print("-" * 40)
                count += 1

        if count == 0:
            print("⚠️ 未找到支持 generateContent 的模型。")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f" 查询失败: {e}")
==================== END FILE: tools/check_models.py ====================


==================== START FILE: tools/code_backup.py ====================
# tools/code_backup.py
"""
代码工程一键备份 / 还原工具（带进度显示 + 真·时光倒流）

使用方式（在项目根目录）：
1) 备份当前代码：
   python tools/code_backup.py backup

2) 还原代码到某个历史快照：
   python tools/code_backup.py restore

说明：
- 仅针对「代码工程」做快照，不含数据库内容。
- 会忽略 backup/output/logs/__pycache__/.git/.venv 等目录。
- 还原时的语义：
    1) 先自动备份当前工程到一个新快照（防后悔）
    2) 删除当前工程中所有非忽略的文件和目录
    3) 再把目标快照完全展开回到项目根目录
  ==> 恢复结束后，工程代码 = 当时快照状态，多出来的新文件会被删除。
"""

import os
import sys
import shutil
import zipfile
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

# ============= 基础路径 =============
BASE_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent  # 项目根目录
BACKUP_ROOT = BASE_DIR / "backup" / "code_snapshots"
BACKUP_ROOT.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# 忽略的目录/文件名（只匹配顶层目录名）
EXCLUDE_DIRS = {
    "backup",        # 备份目录本身
    "output",
    "logs",
    "__pycache__",
    ".git",
    ".venv",
    ".idea",
    ".pytest_cache",
}
EXCLUDE_FILES = {
    ".DS_Store",
}

# ============= 通用工具函数 =============

def _should_exclude(path: Path) -> bool:
    """
    判断某个路径在备份/清理时是否应被忽略
    """
    rel = path.relative_to(BASE_DIR)

    # 排除隐藏目录/文件（以 . 开头），但保留 .env
    for part in rel.parts:
        if part.startswith(".") and part not in {".env"}:
            return True

    # 顶层目录过滤
    if rel.parts and rel.parts[0] in EXCLUDE_DIRS:
        return True

    # 文件名过滤
    if path.name in EXCLUDE_FILES:
        return True

    return False


def _print_progress(current: int, total: int, prefix: str = ""):
    """
    简单文本进度条，用于终端显示。
    """
    if total == 0:
        percent = 100
    else:
        percent = int(current / total * 100)

    bar_len = 30
    filled_len = int(bar_len * percent / 100)

    bar = "█" * filled_len + "-" * (bar_len - filled_len)
    print(f"\r{prefix} |{bar}| {percent:3d}%", end="", flush=True)

    if current >= total:
        print()  # 换行


# ============= 1. 创建快照 =============

def _collect_files_for_backup():
    """
    收集需要备份的所有文件列表（先收集再打包，方便统计总数做进度）
    """
    print("🔍 正在扫描需要备份的文件...")
    files = []
    for root, dirs, filenames in os.walk(BASE_DIR):
        root_path = Path(root)
        rel_root = root_path.relative_to(BASE_DIR)

        # 顶层目录过滤
        if rel_root.parts and rel_root.parts[0] in EXCLUDE_DIRS:
            dirs[:] = []  # 不再深入该目录
            continue

        for name in filenames:
            file_path = root_path / name
            if _should_exclude(file_path):
                continue
            files.append(file_path)

    print(f"📂 需要备份的文件数：{len(files)}")
    return files


def create_snapshot(label: str = "") -> Path:
    """
    创建当前代码的 zip 快照，返回生成的文件路径

    label: 可选标签，例如 "pre_restore" 方便辨认。
    """
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
    if label:
        zip_name = f"code_snapshot_{timestamp}_{label}.zip"
    else:
        zip_name = f"code_snapshot_{timestamp}.zip"

    zip_path = BACKUP_ROOT / zip_name

    files = _collect_files_for_backup()
    total = len(files)

    print(f"📦 正在创建代码快照：{zip_path}")
    processed = 0

    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, "w", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zf:
        for file_path in files:
            rel_path = file_path.relative_to(BASE_DIR)
            zf.write(file_path, arcname=str(rel_path))

            processed += 1
            _print_progress(processed, total, prefix="📦 备份进度")

    print(" 代码快照创建完成！")
    return zip_path


# ============= 2. 列出快照 =============

def list_snapshots():
    """
    列出所有已有快照，按时间排序（最新在后）
    """
    snaps = sorted(
        [p for p in BACKUP_ROOT.glob("code_snapshot_*.zip") if p.is_file()],
        key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime
    )
    return snaps


# ============= 3. 还原相关：清理 + 解压 + 覆盖 =============

def _collect_paths_for_cleanup():
    """
    收集需要删除的文件和目录（不含 EXCLUDE_DIRS & 隐藏目录等）
    返回: (files, dirs)
        files: 所有要删除的文件 Path 列表
        dirs : 所有要删除的目录 Path 列表（从子目录到父目录）
    """
    files = []
    dirs = []

    print("🔍 正在扫描需要清理的现有文件...")

    # bottom-up 遍历，方便之后删除空目录
    for root, dirnames, filenames in os.walk(BASE_DIR, topdown=False):
        root_path = Path(root)
        rel_root = root_path.relative_to(BASE_DIR)

        # 顶层在忽略列表里的目录直接跳过
        if rel_root.parts and rel_root.parts[0] in EXCLUDE_DIRS:
            continue

        # 文件
        for name in filenames:
            file_path = root_path / name
            if _should_exclude(file_path):
                continue
            files.append(file_path)

        # 目录（除了 BASE_DIR 自身）
        if root_path != BASE_DIR and not _should_exclude(root_path):
            dirs.append(root_path)

    print(f"📂 准备删除的文件数：{len(files)}，目录数：{len(dirs)}")
    return files, dirs


def _cleanup_current_project():
    """
    删除当前工程中所有非忽略的文件和目录。
    """
    files, dirs = _collect_paths_for_cleanup()

    # 删除文件
    total_files = len(files)
    print("🧹 正在删除现有文件...")
    for i, file_path in enumerate(files, start=1):
        try:
            file_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"\n⚠️ 删除文件失败: {file_path} ({e})")
        _print_progress(i, total_files, prefix="🧹 删除文件")

    # 删除空目录（从子目录开始）
    total_dirs = len(dirs)
    print("🧹 正在删除空目录...")
    for i, dir_path in enumerate(dirs, start=1):
        try:
            # 只删除已经空掉的目录，避免误删还在用的
            if dir_path.exists() and not any(dir_path.iterdir()):
                dir_path.rmdir()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"\n⚠️ 删除目录失败: {dir_path} ({e})")
        _print_progress(i, total_dirs, prefix="🧹 删除目录")

    print(" 清理完成。")


def _extract_snapshot_to_temp(snap_path: Path, temp_dir: Path):
    """
    解压快照到临时目录，带进度显示
    """
    print(f"🧩 正在解压快照：{snap_path.name}")

    with zipfile.ZipFile(snap_path, "r") as zf:
        members = zf.infolist()
        total = len(members)
        processed = 0

        for member in members:
            zf.extract(member, temp_dir)
            processed += 1
            _print_progress(processed, total, prefix="🧩 解压进度")

    print(" 解压完成。")


def _copy_tree_with_progress(src_root: Path, dst_root: Path):
    """
    将 src_root 下所有文件复制到 dst_root（覆盖），带进度显示
    """
    print("📝 正在将快照内容写回当前项目...")

    files = []
    for root, dirs, filenames in os.walk(src_root):
        root_path = Path(root)
        for name in filenames:
            files.append(root_path / name)

    total = len(files)
    processed = 0

    for file_path in files:
        rel = file_path.relative_to(src_root)
        dest_path = dst_root / rel
        dest_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        shutil.copy2(file_path, dest_path)

        processed += 1
        _print_progress(processed, total, prefix="📝 写入进度")

    print(" 写回完成。")


def restore_snapshot():
    """
    从已有快照中选择一个进行还原。

    真·时光倒流流程：
    1) 先自动备份当前代码 -> 生成一个 code_snapshot_..._pre_restore.zip
    2) 清理当前项目中所有非忽略的文件和目录
    3) 解压目标快照到临时目录
    4) 将临时目录的内容完整复制回项目
    """
    snaps = list_snapshots()
    if not snaps:
        print(" 未找到任何代码快照，请先执行 backup 再尝试还原。")
        return

    print("🔁 可用的代码快照如下：")
    for idx, snap in enumerate(snaps, start=1):
        mtime = datetime.fromtimestamp(snap.stat().st_mtime).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
        print(f"{idx}. {snap.name}  (创建时间: {mtime})")

    # 让用户选择一个快照
    while True:
        choice = input(f"请输入要还原的快照序号 (1-{len(snaps)})，或按回车取消：").strip()
        if not choice:
            print("操作已取消。")
            return

        if not choice.isdigit():
            print("请输入数字序号。")
            continue

        idx = int(choice)
        if 1 <= idx <= len(snaps):
            target_snap = snaps[idx - 1]
            break
        else:
            print("序号超出范围，请重新输入。")

    # 二次确认
    print(f"\n⚠️ 警告：即将用快照 [{target_snap.name}] 完全覆盖当前项目代码。")
    print("   该操作会删除当前项目中所有非忽略的文件和目录，无法直接撤销。")
    print("   但系统会在还原前自动再备份一次当前代码。")
    confirm = input("输入 'YES' 以继续还原：").strip()
    if confirm != "YES":
        print("操作已取消。")
        return

    # 0) 先自动备份当前状态
    print("\n🛡 正在为当前代码创建“还原前快照”...")
    pre_snap = create_snapshot(label="pre_restore")
    print(f"🛡 已创建还原前快照：{pre_snap.name}")

    # 1) 清理当前项目
    _cleanup_current_project()

    # 2) 解压目标快照到临时目录
    temp_dir = BACKUP_ROOT / "__restore_temp__"
    if temp_dir.exists():
        shutil.rmtree(temp_dir)
    temp_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    _extract_snapshot_to_temp(target_snap, temp_dir)

    # 3) 将快照内容复制回项目
    _copy_tree_with_progress(temp_dir, BASE_DIR)

    # 4) 清理解压目录
    shutil.rmtree(temp_dir, ignore_errors=True)

    print(" 代码还原完成！当前工程已回到所选快照状态。")
    print("   如需撤销本次还原，可以使用刚才自动创建的 pre_restore 快照再次执行 restore。")


# ============= CLI 入口 =============

def print_usage():
    print("用法：")
    print("  python tools/code_backup.py backup   # 创建当前代码快照")
    print("  python tools/code_backup.py restore  # 从历史快照还原代码（会清理当前代码并自动备份）")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    if len(sys.argv) < 2:
        print_usage()
        sys.exit(0)

    cmd = sys.argv[1].lower()
    if cmd == "backup":
        create_snapshot()
    elif cmd == "restore":
        restore_snapshot()
    else:
        print(f"未知命令: {cmd}")
        print_usage()

==================== END FILE: tools/code_backup.py ====================


==================== START FILE: core/auth_service.py ====================
# core/auth_service.py
import os
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Optional, Dict, Tuple, Any
import pandas as pd

from config import Config
from core.repository.db_client import DBClient
from core.logging_config import get_logger
from core.security import SecurityUtils


@dataclass
class User:
    username: str
    is_admin: bool
    is_locked: bool
    failed_attempts: int
    session_token: str = ""


class AuthService:
    """认证与用户管理服务 (业务逻辑层)"""

    USER_TABLE = "User_Account"
    PERM_TABLE = "User_Permission"
    LOGIN_HISTORY_TABLE = "User_Login_History"
    MAX_FAILED_ATTEMPTS = 10

    _logger = get_logger(__name__)

    @classmethod
    def initialize(cls) -> None:
        cls._ensure_schema()
        cls._bootstrap_default_users()

    @classmethod
    def _ensure_schema(cls) -> None:
        # 1. 确保用户表存在
        sql_user = f"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `{cls.USER_TABLE}` (id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY, username VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL UNIQUE, password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, is_admin TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 0, is_locked TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 0, failed_attempts INT DEFAULT 0, session_token VARCHAR(64), created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET={Config.DB_CHARSET};"
        DBClient.execute_stmt(sql_user)

        # [Fix] 自动迁移：检查是否存在 session_token 字段，不存在则添加 (解决 OperationalError 1054)
        try:
            check_col = f"SHOW COLUMNS FROM `{cls.USER_TABLE}` LIKE 'session_token'"
            if DBClient.read_df(check_col).empty:
                cls._logger.info(f"正在升级数据库架构: 为 {cls.USER_TABLE} 添加 session_token 字段...")
                DBClient.execute_stmt(
                    f"ALTER TABLE `{cls.USER_TABLE}` ADD COLUMN session_token VARCHAR(64) DEFAULT NULL")
        except Exception as e:
            cls._logger.error(f"Schema 自动迁移失败: {e}")

        # 2. 确保权限表存在
        sql_perm = f"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `{cls.PERM_TABLE}` (id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY, username VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL, permission_key VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL, allowed TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 1, created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, UNIQUE KEY uniq_user_perm (username, permission_key)) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET={Config.DB_CHARSET};"
        DBClient.execute_stmt(sql_perm)

        # 3. 确保历史表存在
        sql_hist = f"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `{cls.LOGIN_HISTORY_TABLE}` (id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY, username VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL, ip_address VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL, login_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, INDEX idx_user (username)) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET={Config.DB_CHARSET};"
        DBClient.execute_stmt(sql_hist)

    @classmethod
    def _bootstrap_default_users(cls) -> None:
        au = os.getenv("DEFAULT_ADMIN_USERNAME", "admin")
        ap = os.getenv("DEFAULT_ADMIN_PASSWORD", "1522P")
        cls._ensure_user(au, ap, True)

        nu = os.getenv("DEFAULT_USER_USERNAME", "user")
        np = os.getenv("DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD", "6M130")
        cls._ensure_user(nu, np, False)

    @classmethod
    def _ensure_user(cls, u, p, is_admin):
        df = DBClient.read_df(f"SELECT id, is_admin FROM `{cls.USER_TABLE}` WHERE username=:u", {"u": u})
        if df.empty:
            ph = SecurityUtils.hash_password(p)
            sql = f"INSERT INTO `{cls.USER_TABLE}` (username, password_hash, is_admin) VALUES (:u, :ph, :a)"
            DBClient.execute_stmt(sql, {"u": u, "ph": ph, "a": 1 if is_admin else 0})
        else:
            if bool(df.iloc[0]["is_admin"]) != is_admin:
                DBClient.execute_stmt(f"UPDATE `{cls.USER_TABLE}` SET is_admin=:a WHERE username=:u",
                                      {"u": u, "a": 1 if is_admin else 0})

    @classmethod
    def authenticate(cls, username: str, password: str, ip: str = "-") -> Tuple[bool, Optional[User], str]:
        u = username.strip()
        if not u or not password: return False, None, "请输入账号密码"

        df = DBClient.read_df(f"SELECT * FROM `{cls.USER_TABLE}` WHERE username=:u LIMIT 1", {"u": u})

        if df.empty:
            SecurityUtils.verify_password("dummy", SecurityUtils.hash_password("dummy"))
            cls._logger.warning(f"用户不存在: {u}", extra={"action": "LOGIN_FAIL", "ip": ip})
            return False, None, "用户名或密码错误"

        row = df.iloc[0]
        # 注意: 这里的 session_token 可能为 None，转为空字符串处理
        token = row.get("session_token") or ""
        user = User(row["username"], bool(row["is_admin"]), bool(row["is_locked"]), int(row["failed_attempts"]), token)

        if user.is_locked:
            cls._logger.warning(f"锁定账号尝试登录: {u}", extra={"action": "LOGIN_LOCKED", "ip": ip})
            return False, None, "账号已锁定"

        if not SecurityUtils.verify_password(password, row["password_hash"]):
            new_f = user.failed_attempts + 1
            is_l = 1 if new_f >= cls.MAX_FAILED_ATTEMPTS else 0
            DBClient.execute_stmt(f"UPDATE `{cls.USER_TABLE}` SET failed_attempts=:f, is_locked=:l WHERE username=:u",
                                  {"f": new_f, "l": is_l, "u": u})
            cls._logger.warning(f"密码错误 ({new_f}次): {u}", extra={"action": "LOGIN_FAIL", "ip": ip})
            return False, None, "用户名或密码错误"

        DBClient.execute_stmt(f"UPDATE `{cls.USER_TABLE}` SET failed_attempts=0 WHERE username=:u", {"u": u})
        cls._logger.info(f"登录验证通过: {u}", extra={"action": "AUTH_SUCCESS", "user": u, "ip": ip})
        return True, user, "登录成功"

    @classmethod
    def refresh_session_token(cls, username: str) -> str:
        token = SecurityUtils.generate_token()
        # 这里会执行 UPDATE，如果字段不存在就会报错，但 _ensure_schema 已经在启动时修复了它
        DBClient.execute_stmt(f"UPDATE `{cls.USER_TABLE}` SET session_token=:t WHERE username=:u",
                              {"t": token, "u": username})
        return token

    @classmethod
    def verify_session_token(cls, username: str, local_token: str) -> bool:
        if not username or not local_token: return False
        try:
            df = DBClient.read_df(f"SELECT session_token FROM `{cls.USER_TABLE}` WHERE username=:u", {"u": username})
            if df.empty: return False
            db_token = df.iloc[0]["session_token"]
            return db_token == local_token
        except:
            return False

    @classmethod
    def record_login_event(cls, username: str, ip: str) -> None:
        DBClient.execute_stmt(f"INSERT INTO `{cls.LOGIN_HISTORY_TABLE}` (username, ip_address) VALUES (:u, :ip)",
                              {"u": username, "ip": ip})

    @classmethod
    def get_user_login_stats(cls, username: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        cnt = \
        DBClient.read_df(f"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM `{cls.LOGIN_HISTORY_TABLE}` WHERE username=:u", {"u": username}).iloc[
            0, 0]
        hist = DBClient.read_df(
            f"SELECT ip_address, COUNT(*) as count, MAX(login_at) as last_seen FROM `{cls.LOGIN_HISTORY_TABLE}` WHERE username=:u GROUP BY ip_address ORDER BY count DESC",
            {"u": username})
        return {"total_logins": int(cnt), "ip_history": hist}

    @classmethod
    def list_users(cls) -> pd.DataFrame:
        return DBClient.read_df(
            f"SELECT username, is_admin, is_locked, failed_attempts FROM `{cls.USER_TABLE}` ORDER BY is_admin DESC")

    @classmethod
    def create_user(cls, u, p, is_admin=False) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        if not DBClient.read_df(f"SELECT 1 FROM `{cls.USER_TABLE}` WHERE username=:u",
                                {"u": u}).empty: return False, "用户已存在"
        ph = SecurityUtils.hash_password(p)
        DBClient.execute_stmt(
            f"INSERT INTO `{cls.USER_TABLE}` (username, password_hash, is_admin) VALUES (:u, :ph, :a)",
            {"u": u, "ph": ph, "a": 1 if is_admin else 0})
        return True, "创建成功"

    @classmethod
    def reset_password(cls, u, np) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        ph = SecurityUtils.hash_password(np)
        row = DBClient.execute_stmt(
            f"UPDATE `{cls.USER_TABLE}` SET password_hash=:ph, failed_attempts=0 WHERE username=:u", {"ph": ph, "u": u})
        return (True, "重置成功") if row else (False, "用户不存在")

    @classmethod
    def set_lock_state(cls, u, lock) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        row = DBClient.execute_stmt(f"UPDATE `{cls.USER_TABLE}` SET is_locked=:l WHERE username=:u",
                                    {"l": 1 if lock else 0, "u": u})
        return (True, "更新成功") if row else (False, "用户不存在")

    @classmethod
    def set_permissions(cls, u, pmap):
        DBClient.execute_stmt(f"DELETE FROM `{cls.PERM_TABLE}` WHERE username=:u", {"u": u})
        vals = ", ".join([f"(:u, :k{i}, 1)" for i in range(len(pmap))])
        if vals: DBClient.execute_stmt(
            f"INSERT INTO `{cls.PERM_TABLE}` (username, permission_key, allowed) VALUES {vals}",
            {"u": u, **{f"k{i}": k for i, k in enumerate(pmap)}})

    @classmethod
    def get_permissions(cls, u) -> Dict[str, bool]:
        df = DBClient.read_df(f"SELECT permission_key FROM `{cls.PERM_TABLE}` WHERE username=:u AND allowed=1",
                              {"u": u})
        return {r["permission_key"]: True for _, r in df.iterrows()}
==================== END FILE: core/auth_service.py ====================


==================== START FILE: core/logging_config.py ====================
# core/logging_config.py

"""
统一日志配置中心 (Enterprise Logging Center)

修改说明:
- 增强 UserLoggerAdapter，确保从 core/context 中获取最新的 user 和 ip 字段。
"""

import logging
import logging.handlers
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any

from config import Config
from core.context import get_context  # <-- 导入 get_context


# ==============================================================================
# 1. 扩展字段安全兜底 Filter
# ==============================================================================

class SafeExtraFilter(logging.Filter):
    """
    确保日志记录对象一定包含以下字段：
    - user, action, table, rows, ip, module_name
    """

    DEFAULTS: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "user": "-",
        "action": "-",
        "table": "-",
        "rows": 0,
        "ip": "-",  # IP 兜底
    }

    def filter(self, record: logging.LogRecord) -> bool:
        for key, default in self.DEFAULTS.items():
            if not hasattr(record, key):
                setattr(record, key, default)

        if not hasattr(record, "module_name"):
            record.module_name = record.name
        return True


# ==============================================================================
# 2. 初始化主日志系统 (保持不变)
# ==============================================================================

_LOG_INITIALIZED = False


def _ensure_log_dir() -> Path:
    """确保日志目录存在"""
    log_dir = Path(Config.LOG_DIR)
    log_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    return log_dir


def init_logging(app_name: str = "EaglestarERP") -> None:
    """
    初始化全局日志配置，只执行一次。
    """
    global _LOG_INITIALIZED
    if _LOG_INITIALIZED:
        return

    log_dir = _ensure_log_dir()

    # 根 logger 基础配置 (略)
    root_logger = logging.getLogger()
    root_logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    root_logger.handlers.clear()

    # 公共 Formatter（带业务字段）
    fmt = (
        "%(asctime)s | %(levelname)-8s | %(module_name)s | "
        "user=%(user)s | action=%(action)s | table=%(table)s | rows=%(rows)s | ip=%(ip)s | "  # <-- IP 字段
        "%(message)s"
    )
    datefmt = "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
    formatter = logging.Formatter(fmt=fmt, datefmt=datefmt)

    # 安全兜底 Filter
    safe_filter = SafeExtraFilter()

    # 控制台 Handler (略)
    console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
    console_handler.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    console_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
    console_handler.addFilter(safe_filter)
    root_logger.addHandler(console_handler)

    # 应用日志文件 Handler (略)
    app_log_path = log_dir / "app.log"
    file_handler = logging.handlers.RotatingFileHandler(
        filename=str(app_log_path),
        maxBytes=10 * 1024 * 1024,
        backupCount=5,
        encoding="utf-8"
    )
    file_handler.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
    file_handler.addFilter(safe_filter)
    root_logger.addHandler(file_handler)

    # 数据库审计专用 Logger (略)
    db_logger = logging.getLogger("db.audit")
    db_logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)

    db_log_path = log_dir / "db_audit.log"
    db_file_handler = logging.handlers.RotatingFileHandler(
        filename=str(db_log_path),
        maxBytes=20 * 1024 * 1024,
        backupCount=10,
        encoding="utf-8"
    )
    db_file_handler.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    db_file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
    db_file_handler.addFilter(safe_filter)

    db_logger.handlers.clear()
    db_logger.addHandler(db_file_handler)
    db_logger.propagate = False

    _LOG_INITIALIZED = True


# 模块导入时自动初始化一次
init_logging()


# ==============================================================================
# 3. 对外工具函数：获取 Logger (注入 IP)
# ==============================================================================

class UserLoggerAdapter(logging.LoggerAdapter):
    """
    简单的 LoggerAdapter：在 log 调用时自动注入 user 和 ip 字段。
    """

    def __init__(self, logger: logging.Logger):
        super().__init__(logger, {})

    def process(self, msg, kwargs):
        # 从 core/context 实时获取当前用户和 IP
        ctx = get_context()
        current_extra = {"user": ctx.username or "-", "ip": ctx.ip or "-"}

        # 允许在 extra 中继续覆盖/补充字段
        extra = kwargs.get("extra", {})
        merged_extra = {**current_extra, **(extra or {})}
        kwargs["extra"] = merged_extra

        return msg, kwargs


def get_logger(name: Optional[str] = None) -> logging.Logger:
    """
    获取应用 Logger。
    现在不需要传递 user 参数，因为它从 contextvars 中自动获取。
    """
    init_logging()
    logger = logging.getLogger(name if name else "app")
    # 始终使用 Adapter 来注入当前上下文
    return UserLoggerAdapter(logger)


def get_db_audit_logger() -> logging.Logger:
    """
    获取数据库审计 Logger (它会自动从 contextvars 中获取 user 和 ip)。
    """
    init_logging()
    logger = logging.getLogger("db.audit")
    return UserLoggerAdapter(logger)  # 同样使用 Adapter
==================== END FILE: core/logging_config.py ====================

# core/security.py
import os
import base64
import hashlib
import hmac
import uuid

class SecurityUtils:
    """
    [底层组件] 安全加密工具箱
    职责：提供无状态的密码哈希、校验与令牌生成。
    """

    @staticmethod
    def hash_password(password: str) -> str:
        """PBKDF2-SHA256 哈希"""
        if not password: raise ValueError("密码不能为空")
        salt = os.urandom(16)
        iterations = 120000
        dk = hashlib.pbkdf2_hmac("sha256", password.encode("utf-8"), salt, iterations)
        salt_b64 = base64.b64encode(salt).decode("ascii")
        hash_b64 = base64.b64encode(dk).decode("ascii")
        return f"pbkdf2_sha256${iterations}${salt_b64}${hash_b64}"

    @staticmethod
    def verify_password(password: str, stored_hash: str) -> bool:
        """校验密码"""
        try:
            alg, iter_str, salt_b64, hash_b64 = stored_hash.split("$")
            if alg != "pbkdf2_sha256": return False
            salt = base64.b64decode(salt_b64.encode("ascii"))
            stored_dk = base64.b64decode(hash_b64.encode("ascii"))
            dk = hashlib.pbkdf2_hmac("sha256", password.encode("utf-8"), salt, int(iter_str))
            return hmac.compare_digest(dk, stored_dk)
        except Exception:
            return False

    @staticmethod
    def generate_token() -> str:
        """生成唯一会话令牌"""
        return str(uuid.uuid4())
==================== END FILE: core/security.py ====================


==================== START FILE: core/rules.py ====================
# core/rules.py
from config import Config


class BusinessRules:
    """
    [业务规则层]
    集中管理所有硬编码的业务逻辑（如耗损率计算、ABC分类标准）。
    防止这些逻辑散落在各个 .py 文件中导致维护困难。
    """

    @staticmethod
    def get_net_quantity(original_qty: int, action: str) -> float:
        """
        根据 Action 类型，计算扣除耗损后的净销量。

        Args:
            original_qty (int): 原始订单数量
            action (str): 订单动作代码 (CA, RE, CC, CR, PD, etc.)

        Returns:
            float: 净销量

        Reference:
            Config.LOSS_RATES 定义了各类动作的耗损百分比。
        """
        action = str(action).strip().upper()
        rates = Config.LOSS_RATES

        loss_rate = 0.0

        # 具体的业务映射逻辑
        if action == 'CA':
            loss_rate = 1.0  # 取消订单，全额扣除
        elif action == 'RE':
            loss_rate = rates.get('RETURN', 0.3)
        elif action == 'CC':
            loss_rate = rates.get('CASE', 0.6)
        elif action == 'CR':
            loss_rate = rates.get('REQUEST', 0.5)
        elif action == 'PD':
            loss_rate = rates.get('DISPUTE', 1.0)

        # 计算净值： 数量 * (1 - 耗损率)
        return original_qty * (1 - loss_rate)

    @staticmethod
    def get_abc_grade(cumulative_ratio: float) -> tuple[str, float]:
        """
        根据累计销售额占比，返回 ABC 等级和对应的服务水平。

        Returns:
            (Grade, ServiceLevel)
            e.g. ("A", 0.98)
        """
        if cumulative_ratio <= 0.80:
            return "A", 0.98
        elif cumulative_ratio <= 0.95:
            return "B", 0.95
        else:
            return "C", 0.90
==================== END FILE: core/rules.py ====================
