# core/services/diagnostics/sku.py
import pandas as pd
from .base import BaseDiagnostician


class SkuDiagnostician(BaseDiagnostician):
    """
    [策略服务] SKU 供应链健康度诊断专家

    核心关注：库存周转(Turnover)、资金效率(Cash Flow)、供应链风险(Supply Chain Risk)。
    逻辑复刻：Analysis_Performance_SKU.py
    """

    def __init__(self, metrics_cur: dict, metrics_prev: dict, inventory_map: dict):
        super().__init__(metrics_cur, metrics_prev)
        self.inventory_map = inventory_map  # SKU 独有的库存数据

    def _prepare_features(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        data = []
        for sku, cur in self.m_cur.items():
            # 1. 基础财务指标
            sales = cur.get("net_qty", 0)
            rev = cur.get("total_rev", 0)
            profit = cur.get("profit", 0)
            margin = profit / rev if rev > 0 else 0

            # 2. 风险指标 (退货与广告)
            # 退货率 = (Return + Request + Claim) / Total Orders
            # 严格依据
            bad_qty = (cur.get("return_qty", 0) + cur.get("request_qty", 0) + cur.get("claim_qty", 0))
            total_qty = cur.get("total_qty", 0)
            ret_rate = bad_qty / total_qty if total_qty > 0 else 0

            ad_cost = cur.get("net_ad_fee", 0)
            acos = ad_cost / rev if rev > 0 else 0

            # 3. 趋势指标 (环比增长)
            prev_sales = self.m_prev.get(sku, {}).get("net_qty", 0)
            if prev_sales > 0:
                growth = (sales - prev_sales) / prev_sales
            else:
                growth = 1.0 if sales > 0 else 0.0

            # 4. 供应链指标 (DOS - Days of Supply)
            curr_inv = self.inventory_map.get(sku, 0)
            # 假设月销均摊到30天，若销量为0，周转天数设为极值999
            daily_sales = sales / 30 if sales > 0 else 0
            dos = curr_inv / daily_sales if daily_sales > 0 else 999

            data.append({
                "SKU": sku, "Sales": sales, "Margin": margin,
                "ACOS": acos, "ReturnRate": ret_rate,
                "Growth": growth, "DOS": dos, "Inventory": curr_inv
            })

        return pd.DataFrame(data)

    def diagnose(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        df = self._prepare_features()
        if df.empty: return df

        # 动态分位数计算 (BCG矩阵核心)
        q_sales_high = df["Sales"].quantile(0.8)
        q_sales_low = df["Sales"].quantile(0.2)
        q_margin_high = df["Margin"].quantile(0.8)
        q_margin_low = df["Margin"].quantile(0.2)

        results = []
        for _, row in df.iterrows():
            tags, sugs = [], []

            # --- BCG 产品矩阵 ---
            #
            if row["Sales"] > q_sales_high:
                if row["Margin"] > q_margin_high:
                    tags.append("🌟明星(Star)")
                    sugs.append("核心资产: 确保库存优先供应，建立防御壁垒。")
                else:
                    tags.append("🐮现金牛(Cow)")
                    sugs.append("资金支柱: 严控成本，维持现有规模，作为引流入口。")
            elif row["Sales"] < q_sales_low:
                if row["Margin"] < q_margin_low:
                    tags.append("🐕瘦狗(Dog)")
                    sugs.append("负资产: 建议立即停止补货，进行清仓或淘汰。")
                else:
                    tags.append("💎潜力(Question)")
                    sugs.append("观察期: 优化Listing质量，尝试精准广告投放测试。")
            else:
                tags.append("🔹平庸(Average)")
                sugs.append("维持现状: 定期复盘，寻找突破机会。")

            # --- 趋势监控 ---
            #
            if row["Growth"] > 0.2:
                tags.append("🚀飙升")
            elif row["Growth"] < -0.2:
                tags.append("📉衰退")

            # --- 风险预警 ---
            #
            if row["ReturnRate"] > 0.1:
                tags.append("⚠️高退货")
                sugs.append("品质红线: 立即检查产品质量或Listing描述准确性。")

            if row["ACOS"] > 0.4:
                tags.append("🔥广告黑洞")
                sugs.append("ROI过低: 缩减广告预算，优化关键词匹配。")

            # --- 库存健康度 (DOS) ---
            #
            if row["DOS"] < 7:
                tags.append("🚨断货预警")
                sugs.append("紧急补货: 库存不足支撑一周销量，需空运补货。")
            elif row["DOS"] > 180:
                tags.append("📦滞销积压")
                sugs.append("去库存: 库龄过长，建议站外Deal或降价清仓。")

            results.append({
                "SKU": row["SKU"],
                "诊断标签": " | ".join(tags),
                "AI运营建议": " ".join(sugs),
                "销量": int(row["Sales"]),
                "利润率": f"{row['Margin']:.2%}",
                "ACOS": f"{row['ACOS']:.2%}",
                "周转天数": round(row["DOS"], 1),
                "退货率": f"{row['ReturnRate']:.2%}",
                "当前库存": int(row["Inventory"])
            })

        return pd.DataFrame(results)

    @staticmethod
    def get_tag_definitions() -> list:
        return [
            "📘 SKU 供应链诊断体系说明 (Supply Chain Diagnostics):",
            "=================================================================================",
            "1. 【BCG 矩阵定位】 基于本期数据分位数(Quantile)动态划分:",
            "   - 🌟 明星 (Star)     [销量Top20% + 利润Top20%] : 企业增长引擎，需资源倾斜。",
            "   - 🐮 现金牛 (Cow)    [销量Top20% + 利润非Top]  : 市场占有率高，提供稳定现金流。",
            "   - 💎 潜力 (Question) [销量Bottom20% + 利润Top] : 高毛利但在孵化期，需流量扶持。",
            "   - 🐕 瘦狗 (Dog)      [销量Bottom20% + 利润Bottom] : 滞销且亏损，应剥离资产。",
            "",
            "2. 【库存健康度 (DOS)】 Days of Supply:",
            "   - 🚨 断货预警 (DOS < 7天): 极高缺货风险，可能导致Listing降权。",
            "   - 📦 滞销积压 (DOS > 180天): 资金周转效率极低，需计提跌价准备。",
            "",
            "3. 【风险控制】:",
            "   - 🔥 广告黑洞 (ACOS > 40%): 广告花费超过警戒线，即使出单也可能亏损。",
            "   - ⚠️ 高退货 (Rate > 10%): 产品存在质量或描述缺陷，甚至导致封号风险。",
            "================================================================================="
        ]
==================== END FILE: core/services/diagnostics/sku.py ====================


==================== START FILE: core/services/diagnostics/crm.py ====================
# core/services/diagnostics/crm.py

import pandas as pd
from .base import BaseDiagnostician


class CustomerDiagnostician(BaseDiagnostician):
    """
    [策略服务] 客户价值与风险诊断专家 (CRM Professional)

    V2.0 Fix:
    1. 显式实现 __init__ 以匹配 BaseDiagnostician 接口。
    2. 将传入的 metrics_cur (DataFrame) 正确赋值给 self.m_cur。
    """

    def __init__(self, metrics_cur: pd.DataFrame, metrics_prev: pd.DataFrame = None, **kwargs):
        """
        初始化诊断器
        :param metrics_cur: 本期 RFM 数据 (DataFrame)
        :param metrics_prev: 上期数据 (CRM 暂未使用，设为 None)
        """
        # 必须显式调用父类初始化，或者手动赋值
        # 这里我们手动赋值以确保类型安全，因为基类可能期望的是 dict，但 CRM 传的是 DataFrame
        self.m_cur = metrics_cur
        self.m_prev = metrics_prev
        self.kwargs = kwargs

    def diagnose(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        # 在 CRM 中，m_cur 是一个 DataFrame，不是 dict
        df = self.m_cur.copy()
        if df.empty: return df

        # 计算动态阈值 (Top 20%)
        q_net_m_high = df["Net_Monetary"].quantile(0.8)
        q_freq_high = df["Frequency"].quantile(0.8)

        results = []

        for _, row in df.iterrows():
            tags, sugs = [], []

            # 提取核心指标
            user = row["buyer username"]
            freq = row["Frequency"]
            net_monetary = row["Net_Monetary"]  # 核心指标：净值
            gross_monetary = row["Gross_Monetary"]
            recency = row["Recency"]
            ret_rate = row["ReturnRate"]
            dispute = row["DisputeCount"]
            aov = row["AOV"]

            is_target_user = False

            # 基础安全判定: 退货率 < 20% 且 无纠纷
            is_safe_user = (ret_rate < 0.2) and (dispute == 0)

            # =========================================================
            # 1. 劣质/风险组 (Risk Group)
            # =========================================================

            # 规则A: 纠纷黑名单
            if dispute > 0:
                tags.append("纠纷发起者")
                sugs.append("高危预警: 曾发起Payment Dispute，建议拉黑。")
                is_target_user = True

            # 规则B: 惯性退货 (买得多退得多)
            if freq >= 2 and ret_rate > 0.3:
                tags.append("⚠️惯性退货")
                sugs.append(f"利润杀手: 退货率{ret_rate:.0%}，实际净值仅{net_monetary:.2f}。")
                is_target_user = True

            # 规则C: 虚假大户 (Gross很高，Net很低)
            if gross_monetary > 1000 and (net_monetary / gross_monetary) < 0.2:
                tags.append("🤡虚假大户")
                sugs.append("无效交易: 产生大量流水但无实际利润，浪费运费。")
                is_target_user = True

            # =========================================================
            # 2. 优质/价值组 (Value Group)
            # =========================================================

            if is_safe_user:
                # 规则D: 超级鲸鱼 (Real Whale)
                if net_monetary > df["Net_Monetary"].quantile(0.9):
                    tags.append("🐳超级鲸鱼")
                    sugs.append("VVIP: 净贡献极高，需防止流失。")
                    is_target_user = True

                # 规则E: 忠诚铁粉 (Loyalist)
                elif freq >= 4 and recency < 60:
                    tags.append("❤️忠诚铁粉")
                    sugs.append("高粘性: 复购习惯良好，新品推广首选。")
                    is_target_user = True

                # 规则F: 潜力批发商 (Wholesaler)
                elif aov > 500 and freq <= 5:
                    tags.append("📦潜力批发商")
                    sugs.append("B端开发: 单笔净值高，可能是线下店或同行。")
                    is_target_user = True

                # 规则G: 沉睡大客户
                elif net_monetary > q_net_m_high and recency > 90:
                    tags.append("💤沉睡大客户")
                    sugs.append("召回: 优质客户流失预警，建议邮件触达。")
                    is_target_user = True

            if not is_target_user:
                continue

            results.append({
                "买家用户名": user,
                "客户标签": " | ".join(tags),
                "运营建议": " ".join(sugs),
                "净消费额(Net LTV)": round(net_monetary, 2),
                "总流水(Gross)": round(gross_monetary, 2),
                "订单数(1Y)": freq,
                "退货率(1Y)": f"{ret_rate:.1%}",
                "最近购买(天前)": int(recency),
                "客单价(Net AOV)": round(aov, 2)
            })

        return pd.DataFrame(results)

    @staticmethod
    def get_tag_definitions() -> list:
        return [
            "📘 客户价值与风险诊断说明 (CRM V2.0):",
            "=================================================================================",
            "【核心逻辑】 数据基于【过去365天】。所有价值判断基于【净消费额 (Net LTV)】，即扣除退款后的真实收入。",
            "",
            "1. 🚫 风险控制:",
            "   -  纠纷发起者: 有 Payment Dispute 记录。",
            "   - ⚠️ 惯性退货: 购买>=2次 且 退货率>30%。",
            "   - 🤡 虚假大户: 总流水高，但净值极低 (退款占比>80%)，属于无效繁荣。",
            "",
            "2. 💎 价值挖掘 (前提: 退货率<20%):",
            "   - 🐳 超级鲸鱼: 净消费额处于全店 Top 10%。",
            "   - ❤️ 忠诚铁粉: 年购买>=4次 且 最近60天有交易。",
            "   - 📦 潜力批发商: 购买频次低，但单笔净值 > $500。",
            "   - 💤 沉睡大客户: 历史净值高(Top 20%) 但 >90天未回购。",
            "================================================================================="
        ]
==================== END FILE: core/services/diagnostics/crm.py ====================


==================== START FILE: core/services/diagnostics/logistics.py ====================
# core/services/diagnostics/logistics.py
import pandas as pd
from .base import BaseDiagnostician


class LogisticsDiagnostician(BaseDiagnostician):
    """
    [策略服务] 物流效益诊断专家 (Logistics Efficiency)

    核心关注：物流费效比、异常费用管控、渠道利润。
    """

    def diagnose(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        df = self.m_cur.copy()
        if df.empty: return df

        results = []
        for _, row in df.iterrows():
            tags, sugs = [], []

            # 提取核心指标
            combo = row["Combo"]
            total_shipping_cost = row["总物流成本"]
            total_rev = row["总销售额"]

            # 细分费用
            base_cost = row["原始邮费"]
            penalty = row["邮费罚款"]
            overpay = row["超支邮费"]
            return_ship = row["包邮退货邮费"]

            # 收入端 (假设 Order Earning 中的 Shipping label-Earning data 是平台扣除的，
            # 这里我们需要逻辑转换：如果有 Shipping Paid by Buyer 数据最好，
            # 暂时用 '物流费率' 判定)

            ship_ratio = total_shipping_cost / total_rev if total_rev > 0 else 0

            # =========================================================
            # 1. 异常管控 (Cost Control)
            # =========================================================

            # 规则A: 罚款黑洞
            # 罚款金额 > 原始邮费的 20%
            if base_cost > 0 and (penalty / base_cost) > 0.2:
                tags.append("💸罚款黑洞")
                sugs.append("尺寸/重量异常: 实际发货规格与申报严重不符，请复核仓库SOP。")

            # 规则B: 超支预警 (Underpaid)
            if overpay > 5:  # 绝对值大于5刀
                tags.append("⚖️重量超支")
                sugs.append("渠道错配: 可能使用了不适合该重量段的物流服务。")

            # 规则C: 退货运费杀手
            if return_ship > (total_shipping_cost * 0.3):
                tags.append("↩️退货运费杀手")
                sugs.append("退货损耗高: 大量物流费浪费在退货面单上。")

            # =========================================================
            # 2. 效益分析 (Efficiency)
            # =========================================================

            # 规则D: 极致物流 (High Efficiency)
            # 物流费率 < 10% (对于大件/重货很难得)
            if ship_ratio < 0.10 and total_shipping_cost > 0:
                tags.append("极致物流")
                sugs.append("优秀模型: 该组合物流成本控制极佳，具有定价优势。")

            # 规则E: 利润侵蚀 (High Cost)
            # 物流费率 > 30%
            if ship_ratio > 0.30:
                tags.append("🩸利润侵蚀")
                sugs.append("运费过高: 运费占售价30%以上，建议提价或更换海外仓/物流商。")

            if not tags:
                tags.append("🔹正常")

            results.append({
                "Combo组合": combo,
                "物流诊断": " | ".join(tags),
                "优化建议": " ".join(sugs),
                "总单量": int(row["原始单数"]),
                "物流费率": f"{ship_ratio:.1%}",
                "总运费": round(total_shipping_cost, 2),
                "罚款占比": f"{(penalty / base_cost):.1%}" if base_cost > 0 else "0.0%"
            })

        # 按 总运费 降序，优先看花钱最多的
        return pd.DataFrame(results).sort_values("总运费", ascending=False)

    @staticmethod
    def get_tag_definitions() -> list:
        return [
            "📘 物流效益诊断说明 (Logistics Diagnostics):",
            "=================================================================================",
            "1. 【异常管控 (Cost Control)】:",
            "   - 💸 罚款黑洞: 罚款金额超过基础运费的20%。通常因尺寸测量错误或重量少报导致。",
            "   - ⚖️ 重量超支: 存在 Underpaid 补缴记录，需校准电子秤或更新产品参数。",
            "   - ↩️ 退货运费杀手: 退货产生的面单费用占总运费30%以上。",
            "",
            "2. 【费效比分析 (Efficiency)】:",
            "   -  极致物流: 物流费率 < 10%。该产品具有极强的物流成本优势，适合做爆款。",
            "   - 🩸 利润侵蚀: 物流费率 > 30%。运费吃掉了大部分利润，建议提价或优化包装体积。",
            "================================================================================="
        ]

==================== START FILE: core/services/diagnostics/listing.py ====================
# core/services/diagnostics/listing.py
import pandas as pd
from .base import BaseDiagnostician


class ListingDiagnostician(BaseDiagnostician):
    """
    [策略服务] Listing (Item ID) 销售表现诊断专家

    核心关注：链接权重(Weight)、流量价值(Traffic Value)、生命周期(Lifecycle)。
    逻辑复刻：Analysis_Performance_Listing.py
    """

    def diagnose(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        data = []
        for iid, cur in self.m_cur.items():
            sales = cur.get("net_qty", 0)
            rev = cur.get("total_rev", 0)
            profit = cur.get("profit", 0)
            margin = profit / rev if rev > 0 else 0

            ad_cost = cur.get("net_ad_fee", 0)
            acos = ad_cost / rev if rev > 0 else 0

            # 环比增长
            prev_sales = self.m_prev.get(iid, {}).get("net_qty", 0)
            if prev_sales > 0:
                growth = (sales - prev_sales) / prev_sales
            else:
                growth = 1.0 if sales > 0 else 0.0

            # 退货率 (Listing 维度的退货更反映描述不符问题)
            total_qty = cur.get("total_qty", 0)
            bad_qty = cur.get("return_qty", 0) + cur.get("claim_qty", 0)
            ret_rate = bad_qty / total_qty if total_qty > 0 else 0

            data.append({
                "item id": iid,
                "item title": cur.get("title", ""),
                "Sales": sales, "Margin": margin,
                "ACOS": acos, "Growth": growth, "ReturnRate": ret_rate
            })

        df = pd.DataFrame(data)
        if df.empty: return df

        q_sales_high = df["Sales"].quantile(0.8)
        q_sales_low = df["Sales"].quantile(0.2)
        q_margin_high = df["Margin"].quantile(0.8)
        q_margin_low = df["Margin"].quantile(0.2)

        results = []
        for _, row in df.iterrows():
            tags, sugs = [], []

            #
            if row["Sales"] > q_sales_high:
                if row["Margin"] > q_margin_high:
                    tags.append("🌟王牌Listing")
                    sugs.append("核心资产: 链接权重极高，防守竞品跟卖。")
                else:
                    tags.append("🐮引流Listing")
                    sugs.append("流量入口: 利用关联销售(Variation/Bundle)带动高利款。")
            elif row["Sales"] < q_sales_low:
                if row["Margin"] < q_margin_low:
                    tags.append("🐕垃圾Listing")
                    sugs.append("沉没成本: 建议下架重做，释放刊登额度。")
                else:
                    tags.append("💎长尾Listing")
                    sugs.append("精准流量: 优化长尾关键词，维持高ROI。")
            else:
                tags.append("🔹腰部Listing")
                sugs.append("潜力挖掘: 分析转化率，尝试参加平台活动。")

            if row["Growth"] > 0.2:
                tags.append("🚀权重上升")
            elif row["Growth"] < -0.2:
                tags.append("📉权重下滑")

            if row["ReturnRate"] > 0.1: tags.append("⚠️高退货风险")
            if row["ACOS"] > 0.4: tags.append("🔥广告亏损")

            results.append({
                "Item ID": row["item id"],
                "Item Title": row["item title"],
                "诊断标签": " | ".join(tags),
                "AI运营建议": " ".join(sugs),
                "销量": int(row["Sales"]),
                "利润率": f"{row['Margin']:.2%}",
                "增长率": f"{row['Growth']:.2%}",
                "ACOS": f"{row['ACOS']:.2%}"
            })
        return pd.DataFrame(results)

    @staticmethod
    def get_tag_definitions() -> list:
        return [
            "📘 Listing 销售表现诊断说明 (Sales Performance):",
            "=================================================================================",
            "1. 【链接分层策略】:",
            "   - 🌟 王牌 (Ace):      高流量转化 + 高溢价能力 -> 品牌护城河。",
            "   - 🐮 引流 (Traffic):  高流量转化 + 低溢价 -> 用于抢占类目排名。",
            "   - 💎 长尾 (Long Tail): 低流量 + 高溢价 -> 满足特定小众需求。",
            "   - 🐕 垃圾 (Trash):    无流量 + 无利润 -> 占用运营精力的负债。",
            "",
            "2. 【运营关键指标】:",
            "   - 🚀 权重上升: 销量环比涨幅 > 20%，建议加大推广力度乘胜追击。",
            "   - 🔥 广告亏损: ACOS > 40%，需检查是否关键词宽泛匹配导致无效点击。",
            "================================================================================="
        ]
==================== END FILE: core/services/diagnostics/listing.py ====================


==================== START FILE: core/services/diagnostics/combo.py ====================
# core/services/diagnostics/combo.py
import pandas as pd
from .base import BaseDiagnostician


class ComboDiagnostician(BaseDiagnostician):
    """
    [策略服务] Combo (Full SKU) 捆绑策略诊断专家

    核心关注：捆绑有效性(Bundling Efficiency)、连坐风险(Risk Association)。
    逻辑复刻：Analysis_Performance_Combo.py
    """

    def diagnose(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        data = []
        for sku, cur in self.m_cur.items():
            sales = cur.get("net_qty", 0)
            rev = cur.get("total_rev", 0)
            profit = cur.get("profit", 0)
            margin = profit / rev if rev > 0 else 0

            prev_sales = self.m_prev.get(sku, {}).get("net_qty", 0)
            growth = (sales - prev_sales) / prev_sales if prev_sales > 0 else (1.0 if sales > 0 else 0.0)

            # 连坐风险检查
            # 如果 Combo 中有一个子件质量差，会导致整个大金额订单退货
            bad_qty = cur.get("return_qty", 0) + cur.get("claim_qty", 0)
            total_qty = cur.get("total_qty", 0)
            ret_rate = bad_qty / total_qty if total_qty > 0 else 0

            data.append({"full sku": sku, "Sales": sales, "Margin": margin, "Growth": growth, "ReturnRate": ret_rate})

        df = pd.DataFrame(data)
        if df.empty: return df

        q_sales_high = df["Sales"].quantile(0.8)
        q_sales_low = df["Sales"].quantile(0.2)
        q_margin_high = df["Margin"].quantile(0.8)

        results = []
        for _, row in df.iterrows():
            tags, sugs = [], []

            #
            if row["Sales"] > q_sales_high:
                if row["Margin"] > q_margin_high:
                    tags.append("👑黄金组合")
                    sugs.append("策略成功: 捆绑销售成功提升了客单价(AOV)与利润。")
                else:
                    tags.append("📦引流包")
                    sugs.append("走量工具: 通过低价打包抢占市场份额。")
            elif row["Sales"] < q_sales_low:
                tags.append("无效捆绑")
                sugs.append("策略失败: 客户不买账，建议解绑或更换组合方式。")
            else:
                tags.append("🔹普通组合")

            if row["Growth"] > 0.2: tags.append("📈热度上升")

            #
            if row["ReturnRate"] > 0.1:
                tags.append("⚠️连坐风险")
                sugs.append("严重警告: 退货率过高，请排查Combo中是否存在低质量子SKU。")

            results.append({
                "Full SKU": row["full sku"],
                "诊断标签": " | ".join(tags),
                "AI运营建议": " ".join(sugs),
                "销量": int(row["Sales"]),
                "利润率": f"{row['Margin']:.2%}",
                "退货率": f"{row['ReturnRate']:.2%}"
            })
        return pd.DataFrame(results)

    @staticmethod
    def get_tag_definitions() -> list:
        return [
            "📘 Combo 捆绑策略诊断说明 (Bundling Strategy):",
            "=================================================================================",
            "1. 【组合效益分析】:",
            "   - 👑 黄金组合: 1+1>2，成功让客户为高客单价买单，且利润丰厚。",
            "   -  无效捆绑: 1+1<2，客户更倾向于单独购买子产品，打包反而降低了转化。",
            "",
            "2. 【连坐风险 (Cannibalization)】:",
            "   - ⚠️ 连坐风险: 因组合中某一个廉价配件质量差，导致客户退掉整个高价包裹。",
            "                 (例: 赠品螺丝生锈，导致几百刀的轮毂被退货)",
            "================================================================================="
        ]
==================== END FILE: core/services/diagnostics/combo.py ====================


==================== START FILE: core/services/diagnostics/base.py ====================
# core/services/diagnostics/base.py
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
import pandas as pd


class BaseDiagnostician(ABC):
    """
    [接口定义] 诊断专家基类

    企业级规范：所有具体的诊断业务（SKU/Listing/Combo）必须遵循此契约。
    强制要求实现 diagnose() 计算逻辑和 get_tag_definitions() 解释文案。
    """

    def __init__(self, metrics_cur: dict, metrics_prev: dict, **kwargs):
        """
        Args:
            metrics_cur: 本期财务指标字典
            metrics_prev: 上期财务指标字典 (用于环比)
            kwargs: 扩展参数 (如库存映射表)
        """
        self.m_cur = metrics_cur
        self.m_prev = metrics_prev
        self.kwargs = kwargs

    @abstractmethod
    def diagnose(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """执行诊断计算，返回包含标签和建议的 DataFrame"""
        pass

    @staticmethod
    @abstractmethod
    def get_tag_definitions() -> list:
        """返回标签的详细业务定义说明 (用于报表 Footer)"""
        pass
==================== END FILE: core/services/diagnostics/base.py ====================
